(********************************************************************************

 Vertical 2-category of a pseudo double category

 In this file, we show that every pseudo double category `C` gives rise to a
 underlying vertical 2-category. This 2-category is defined as follows:
 - Objects: objects of `C`
 - 1-cells: vertical morphisms in `C`
 - 2-cells: squares in `C` whose horizontal sides are identities
 Note that we assume that the associativity and unitality laws in `C` hold
 strictly for vertical morphisms. For this reason, this really is a 2-category
 rather than a bicategory. In addition, if we assume `C` to be a univalent double
 category, then the category of objects and vertical morphisms in `C` is a
 univalent category. The resulting vertical 2-category is then univalent as well:
 it is a univalent category enriched over the category of strict categories.

 In the file `VerticalTwoCategoryStrict.v`, we define the vertical 2-category of
 strict double categories. Most of the development is similar except for how we
 define the composition of 2-cells. Suppose that we have the following diagram in
 a double category

<<
  x --|--> x --|--> x
  |        |        |
  |   s₁   |   s₂   |
  V        V        V
  y --|--> y --|--> y
>>

 Each of the horizontal morphisms in this diagram is an identity. If we perform
 this composition in the vertical 2-category, then we should obtain a square whose
 horizontal sides are identity as well. If we assume our double category to be
 strict, then these horizontal sides in the new square are equal to the identity.
 However, for pseudo double categories, we need to compose it with suitable
 unitors as follows

<<
  x -------|------> x
  |                 |
  |                 |
  V                 V
  x --|--> x --|--> x
  |        |        |
  |   s₁   |   s₂   |
  V        V        V
  y --|--> y --|--> y
  |                 |
  |                 |
  V                 V
  y -------|------> y
>>

 If we compose these squares directly, then the vertical sides of this square
 are composed with the identity on the left. However, since vertical composition
 is strictly unital, we can remove these identities. This explains how composition
 is defined in [underlying_vert_two_cat_data].

 Most of the axioms of 2-categories can be checked directly. The most difficult
 one is associativity. We prove this in `underlying_two_cat_assoc` using several
 lemmas.

 Content
 1. The underlying vertical category
 2. The data of the vertical 2-category
 3. The laws of the vertical 2-category
 4. The vertical 2-category of a pseudo double category

 ********************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.

C: double_cat

v₁, v₂, v₃: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
square v₁ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)

      refine (transportf_square
                (id_v_right _ @ id_v_left _)
                (id_v_right _ @ id_v_left _)
                (linvunitor_h _ ⋆v s₁ ⋆h s₂ ⋆v lunitor_h _)).

  g2

    v₂ : underlying_vert_precategory_data ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧),
   square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x0) (identity_h y0)) x z
    (f · g1) (f · g2)
 exact (λ x y z v w₁ w₂ s, id_h_square v ⋆v s).

    (f1 · g) (f2 · g)
 exact (λ x y z v₁ v₂ w s, s ⋆v id_h_square w).
  Defined.

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (** We prove associativity for 2-cells with a series of lemmata *)
  Section Assoc.
    Context {x y : C}
            {v₁ v₂ v₃ v₄ : x -->v y}
            (s₁ : square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y))
            (s₂ : square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y))
            (s₃ : square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)).

    
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p: v₁ = (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y
q: v₄ = (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y
lassociator_h (identity_h x) (identity_h x)
  (identity_h x) ⋆v s₁ ⋆h s₂ ⋆h s₃
⋆v rassociator_h (identity_h y) (identity_h y)
     (identity_h y) = trfs s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃)

⋆v rassociator_h (identity_h y) (identity_h y)
     (identity_h y) = trfs s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃)

C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y

s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p: (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y =
identity_v x
·v (identity_v x
    ·v (v₁ ·v (identity_v y ·v identity_v y)))
q: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y =
identity_v x
·v (identity_v x
    ·v (v₄ ·v (identity_v y ·v identity_v y)))
id_v_square (identity_h x)
⋆h linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
⋆v (lassociator_h (identity_h x) (identity_h x)
      (identity_h x)
    ⋆v (s₁ ⋆h s₂ ⋆h s₃
        ⋆v (rassociator_h (identity_h y)
              (identity_h y) (identity_h y)
            ⋆v id_v_square (identity_h y)
               ⋆h lunitor_h (identity_h y)))) =
trfs id_v_square (identity_h x)
     ⋆h linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃)
     ⋆v id_v_square (identity_h y)
        ⋆h lunitor_h (identity_h y)

identity_v x
·v (identity_v x
    ·v (v₁ ·v (identity_v y ·v identity_v y)))
q: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y =
identity_v x
·v (identity_v x
    ·v (v₄ ·v (identity_v y ·v identity_v y)))
trfs id_v_square (identity_h x)
     ⋆h linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃)
     ⋆v id_v_square (identity_h y)
        ⋆h lunitor_h (identity_h y) =
trfs id_v_square (identity_h x)
     ⋆h linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃)
     ⋆v id_v_square (identity_h y)
        ⋆h lunitor_h (identity_h y)

p₄: identity_v x ·v (v₄ ·v identity_v y) = v₄
s₃ = trfs (trfs s₃)

v₄ ·v (identity_v y ·v identity_v y) =
identity_v x ·v (v₄ ·v identity_v y)

p₂: (identity_v x ·v v₂) ·v identity_v y = v₂
p₃: (identity_v x ·v v₃) ·v identity_v y = v₃
p₄: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y = v₄
trfs (trfs (trfs s₁)
           ⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
               ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y))) =
trfs (trfs s₁)
     ⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
         ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y))

      
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p₁: (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y = v₁
p₂: (identity_v x ·v v₂) ·v identity_v y = v₂
p₃: (identity_v x ·v v₃) ·v identity_v y = v₃
p₄: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y = v₄
trfs (trfs s₁)
     ⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
         ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)) =
trfs (trfs s₁)
     ⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
         ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y))

      
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p₁: (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y = v₁
p₂: (identity_v x ·v v₂) ·v identity_v y = v₂
p₃: (identity_v x ·v v₃) ·v identity_v y = v₃
p₄: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y = v₄
(trfs s₁)
⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
    ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)) =
(trfs s₁)
⋆h (linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₂ ⋆h s₃
    ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y))

      
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p₁: (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y = v₁
p₂: (identity_v x ·v v₂) ·v identity_v y = v₂
p₃: (identity_v x ·v v₃) ·v identity_v y = v₃
p₄: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y = v₄
trfs s₁ = trfs s₁

      
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂, v₃, v₄: x -->v y
s₁: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
p₁: (identity_v x ·v v₁) ·v identity_v y = v₁
p₂: (identity_v x ·v v₂) ·v identity_v y = v₂
p₃: (identity_v x ·v v₃) ·v identity_v y = v₃
p₄: (identity_v x ·v v₄) ·v identity_v y = v₄
s₁ = s₁

      apply idpath.
    Qed.
  End Assoc.

C: double_cat
∏ (a b : C) (f g h k : a -->v b)
(x : square f g (identity_h a) (identity_h b))
(y : square g h (identity_h a) (identity_h b))
(z : square h k (identity_h a) (identity_h b)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v x
        ⋆h (trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a) ⋆v y ⋆h z
                 ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b))
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a) ⋆v x ⋆h y
              ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b)) ⋆h z
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b)
 
C: double_cat
x, y: C

s₂: square v₂ v₃ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₃: square v₃ v₄ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v s₁

              ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)) ⋆h s₃
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)

s₁: square v w₁ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
s₂: square w₁ w₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)

           ⋆v (s₁ ⋆h s₂
               ⋆v (lunitor_h (identity_h y)
                   ⋆v id_h_square w₃))) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₁ ⋆h s₂
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y) ⋆v id_h_square w₃

C: double_cat
∏ (a b c : C) (f g : a -->v b) (h i : b -->v c)
(x : square f g (identity_h a) (identity_h b))
(y : square h i (identity_h b) (identity_h c)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (x ⋆v id_h_square h) ⋆h (id_h_square g ⋆v y)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h c) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (id_h_square f ⋆v y) ⋆h (x ⋆v id_h_square i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h c)

     ⋆v (s₁ ⋆v id_h_square w₂)
        ⋆h (id_h_square w₁ ⋆v s₂)

     ⋆v (id_h_square v ⋆v s₂)
        ⋆h (s₁ ⋆v id_h_square w₃)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h z)

trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x) ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂ = ?b

C: double_cat
∏ (a b : C) (f g : a -->v b)
(x : square f g (identity_h a) (identity_h b)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (id_h_square (identity_v a) ⋆v x)
        ⋆h idto2mor (id_v_left g)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v idto2mor (id_v_left f) ⋆h x
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b)

        ⋆h idto2mor (id_v_left v₂)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y) =

     ⋆v idto2mor (id_v_left v₁) ⋆h s
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)

C: double_cat
∏ (a b : C) (f g : a -->v b)
(x : square f g (identity_h a) (identity_h b)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (x ⋆v id_h_square (identity_v b))
        ⋆h idto2mor (id_v_right g)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v idto2mor (id_v_right f) ⋆h x
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h b)
 
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂: x -->v y
s: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square (identity_v y))
        ⋆h idto2mor (id_v_right v₂)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v idto2mor (id_v_right v₁) ⋆h s
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)

      
C: double_cat
x, y: C
v₁, v₂: x -->v y
s: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x) (identity_h y)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x)
     ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square (identity_v y))
        ⋆h (trfs id_h_square (v₂ ·v identity_v y))
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y) =

     ⋆v (trfs id_h_square (v₁ ·v identity_v y)) ⋆h s
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h y)

C: double_cat
∏ (a b c d : C) (f : a -->v b) (g : b -->v c)
(h i : c -->v d)
(x : square h i (identity_h c) (identity_h d)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (id_h_square f ⋆v (id_h_square g ⋆v x))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v f g i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v f g h)
        ⋆h (id_h_square (f ·v g) ⋆v x)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d)
 
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
u: x₁ -->v x₂
v: x₂ -->v x₃
w₁, w₂: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square w₁ w₂ (identity_h x₃) (identity_h x₄)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (id_h_square u ⋆v (id_h_square v ⋆v s))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v u v w₂)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v u v w₁)
        ⋆h (id_h_square (u ·v v) ⋆v s)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄)

      
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C

v: x₂ -->v x₃
w₁, w₂: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square w₁ w₂ (identity_h x₃) (identity_h x₄)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (id_h_square u ⋆v (id_h_square v ⋆v s))
        ⋆h (trfs id_h_square (u ·v (v ·v w₂)))
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (trfs id_h_square (u ·v (v ·v w₁)))
        ⋆h (id_h_square (u ·v v) ⋆v s)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄)

      apply idpath.
    
C: double_cat
∏ (a b c d : C) (f : a -->v b) (g h : b -->v c)
(i : c -->v d)
(x : square g h (identity_h b) (identity_h c)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (id_h_square f ⋆v (x ⋆v id_h_square i))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v f h i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v f g i)
        ⋆h (id_h_square f ⋆v x ⋆v id_h_square i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d)
 
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
u: x₁ -->v x₂
v₁, v₂: x₂ -->v x₃
w: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x₂) (identity_h x₃)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (id_h_square u ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square w))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v u v₂ w)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v u v₁ w)
        ⋆h (id_h_square u ⋆v s ⋆v id_h_square w)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄)

      
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
u: x₁ -->v x₂
v₁, v₂: x₂ -->v x₃
w: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square v₁ v₂ (identity_h x₂) (identity_h x₃)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (id_h_square u ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square w))
        ⋆h (trfs id_h_square (u ·v (v₂ ·v w)))
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (trfs id_h_square (u ·v (v₁ ·v w)))
        ⋆h (id_h_square u ⋆v s ⋆v id_h_square w)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄)

     ⋆v (id_h_square u ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square w))
        ⋆h (trfs id_h_square (u ·v (v₂ ·v w)))
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) = ?b

C: double_cat
∏ (a b c d : C) (f g : a -->v b) (h : b -->v c)
(i : c -->v d)
(x : square f g (identity_h a) (identity_h b)),
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v f h i)
        ⋆h (x ⋆v id_h_square h ⋆v id_h_square i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h a)
     ⋆v (x ⋆v id_h_square (h ·v i))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v g h i)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h d)

     ⋆v idto2mor (assocl_v u₁ v w)
        ⋆h (s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄) =
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (s ⋆v id_h_square (v ·v w))
        ⋆h idto2mor (assocl_v u₂ v w)
     ⋆v lunitor_h (identity_h x₄)

u₁, u₂: x₁ -->v x₂
v: x₂ -->v x₃
w: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square u₁ u₂ (identity_h x₁) (identity_h x₂)
trfs linvunitor_h (identity_h x₁)
     ⋆v (trbs runitor_h (identity_h x₁)
              ⋆v (trfs s ⋆v id_h_square (v ·v w))) =
?b

trfs s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w = ?b

        apply idpath.
      
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
u₁, u₂: x₁ -->v x₂
v: x₂ -->v x₃
w: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square u₁ u₂ (identity_h x₁) (identity_h x₂)
trfs s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w =
trfs s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w

      
C: double_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
u₁, u₂: x₁ -->v x₂
v: x₂ -->v x₃
w: x₃ -->v x₄
s: square u₁ u₂ (identity_h x₁) (identity_h x₂)
s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w =
s ⋆v id_h_square v ⋆v id_h_square w

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Defined.

 exact underlying_vert_two_precat.

C: double_cat
x, y: underlying_vert_two_precat
f, g: underlying_vert_two_precat ⟦ x, y ⟧
isaset
  (two_cat_cells (pr1 underlying_vert_two_precat) f g)

      apply isaset_square.
  Defined.
End VerticalCat.
